## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / nonlinear oscillators
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position x, velocity v, and time t. The acceleration in such systems typically depends on restoring forces (functions of x), damping forces (functions of v), and possibly external driving forces (functions of t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force plus linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring force plus damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping dependent on position)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Combined nonlinear restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (general polynomial restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v (multiplicative coupling between position and velocity)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (sinusoidal external driving)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Velocity-dependent terms linear in v → linear energy dissipation or gain (damping/anti-damping)
- Position-dependent coefficient on velocity (e.g., (1-x**2)*v) → amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillators
- Sinusoidal functions of time → external periodic driving forces
- Cubic position terms with opposite sign to linear term → hardening or softening spring nonlinearity (Duffing-type)
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous/conservative system; presence indicates driven system
- Even powers of x in restoring force → broken symmetry in the potential, leading to asymmetric oscillations
- Odd powers of v in damping → nonlinear dissipation that changes character with amplitude

### Candidate 31: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*cos(c4*t) + c5*sin(c6*t+c7)*cos(c8*t)`
Has trig in t, not in x or v.
**Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 32: `(c0*x³*(c1*x+c2)+c3*v+c4)/(c1*x+c2)`
= `c0*x³ + (c3*v+c4)/(c1*x+c2)`
Rational, not sin.
**Candidate 32 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 33: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*cos(c4*t) + c5*v/(c6+t)^5`
Has cos(t) and rational in t. Not sin(x) or sin(v).
**Candidate 33 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 34: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*sin(c3*v+c4) + c5*v + c6*v*cos(c7*t)`
This has `sin(c3*v+c4)` which can represent `sin(v)` (set c3=1, c4=0). Also has `v*cos(c7*t)`. But GT needs `v*sin(x)` and `sin(v)` and `v³`. This has `sin(v)` but not `v*sin(x)` or `v³`. The `v*cos(c7*t)` term depends on t, not x. Cannot match.
**Candidate 34 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 35: `(c0*v+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(c4*x+c5*x³+c6*v+c7*v*cos(c8*t)))/(c2*t+c3)`
= `(c0*v+c1)/(c2*t+c3) + c4*x + c5*x³ + c6*v + c7*v*cos(c8*t)`
Has rational in t. Not sin(x) or sin(v).
**Candidate 35 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 36: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v^c4 + c5*v*cos(c6*t)`
Has `v^c4` (could be v³ with c4=3), `v*cos(c6*t)`. Missing `v*sin(x)` and `sin(v)`.
**Candidate 36 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 37: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*cos(c4*t) + c5*v³`
Has `v³` and `v*cos(t)`. Missing `v*sin(x)` and `sin(v)`.
**Candidate 37 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 38: Same structure as 35.
**Candidate 38 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidates 39-51: All involve combinations of polynomial, cos(t), exp, log, power functions, or trig in t. None have both `sin(v)` and `v*sin(x)`.

**Candidate 39 verdict: [NO MATCH]**
